 Select Sum(Nvl(Dtl.Free_Qty,0)*Dtl.P_Size) From 
 Dtl,Ias_qut_prm_mst Prm                         
									          Where Dtl.Bill_No=
									              And Dtl.Qt_Prm_Ser=Prm.Quot_Ser

       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Cust_L_Nm , Cust_F_Nm ),
                Nvl (Cust_F_Nm , Cust_L_Nm )) cust_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Cust_GRP_L_NM , Cust_GRP_F_NM ),
                Nvl (Cust_GRP_F_NM,Cust_GRP_L_NM )) group_name
  From IAS_CASH_CUSTMR,IAS_CASH_CUSTMR_GRP
 Where IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.Cust_GRP_CODE  = IAS_CASH_CUSTMR_GRP.Cust_GRP_CODE(+) 
And  cust_code Like  Decode(:ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.cust_code,Null,'%',:ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.cust_code||'%') 
And (:Parameter.User_No = 1 OR  nvl(:PARAMETER.SHW_CSHCST_BY_BRN,0) =0 OR
  EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                                        WHERE U_ID =:PARAMETER.USER_NO
                                          AND S_BRN_USR_PRIV.BRN_NO     = IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.BRN_NO
                                          AND NVL(VIEW_FLAG, 1) = 1 
                                          AND ROWNUM <= 1)  ) 
Order By cust_code

UPDATE_SMAN_COMM_AMT_PRC
UPDATE IAS_POS_RT_BILL_DTL SET COMM_AMT_DTL=(NVL(COMM_PER,0) * (I_PRICE - NVL(DIS_AMT_MST,0)  - NVL(DIS_AMT_DTL,0) ) ) / 100  WHERE RT_BILL_NO = :b1  AND NVL(COMM_PER,0) != 0"UPDATE IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST SET COMM_AMT_DTL=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(SUM(I_QTY * NVL(COMM_AMT_DTL,0) ),0),:b1)   FROM IAS_POS_RT_BILL_DTL  WHERE RT_BILL_NO = :b2 ) WHERE RT_BILL_NO = :b3"

SELECT CRLIMIT_TYPE,NVL(INV_DIS_LMT,0),NVL(INV_DIS_LMT_ITM,INV_DIS_LMT),CRLIMIT_PER   FROM PRIVILEGE_FIXED  WHERE U_ID = :b1"
Select customer.c_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_a_name, c_e_name),
                Nvl (c_e_name, c_a_name)) c_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_group_a_name, c_group_e_name),
                Nvl (c_group_e_name, c_group_a_name)) group_name,
       customer.c_a_code a_code
  From customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     customer.c_Group_Code = Customer_Group.c_Group_Code(+) 
  And  customer.c_code Like  Decode(:ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.c_code,Null,'%',:ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.c_code||'%') 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = customer.c_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And c_code = customer.c_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
Order By c_code
Select kgrp_code||' - '||Nvl(kgrp_a_name,kgrp_e_name) ,
       kgrp_code
  From ias_pos_key_brd_grps_mst
   Where extra_keypad_no = :Parameter.extra_keypad

       bank_name 
  From cash_at_bank 
   Where Exists ( Select 1     From priv_cash 
      Where cash_at_bank.bank_no = priv_cash.cash_no
       And cash_type=2
       And u_id=:Parameter.User_no 
       And Nvl(add_flag,0)=1 
       And RowNum <= 1 )
       And bank_no Like 
Decode(:ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.cash_no,Null,'%',:ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.cash_no||'%') 
 Order By bank_no

                       ,Nvl(cr_card_name,cr_card_e_name),Nvl(cr_card_e_name,cr_card_name)) cr_card_name
 From credit_card_types d
  Where d.Machine_No  = :Parameter.Machine_No
  and  exists (select 1 from Ias_Machines m
     where  M.Machine_No_Bank=D.Machine_No_Bank 	      
          and  nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0 )
   Order By d.cr_card_no

       rt_bill_date  ,
       rt_bill_time  ,
       rt_bill_amt   ,
       net_rt_bill   ,
       Ad_Date,
       pr_rep
Select rt_bill_no    ,
       rt_bill_date  ,
       rt_bill_time  ,
       rt_bill_amt   ,
rt_bill_amt+nvl(VAT_AMT,0)-nvl(DISC_AMT,0) net_rt_bill,
       Ad_Date,
       pr_rep
From ias_pos_hst_rt_bill_mst 
Where Nvl(hung,0)= 0
and  To_Date(rt_Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Mst.rt_Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Mst.rt_Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Num_of_days_shw_bills,1)
and ( :Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists (Select 1 From User_R Where U_Id=ias_pos_hst_rt_bill_mst.ad_u_id
                 Connect By Prior U_Id = U_Mng Start With U_Id = :Parameter.User_No) )
Union 
Select rt_bill_no    ,
       rt_bill_date  ,
       rt_bill_time  ,
       rt_bill_amt   ,
rt_bill_amt+nvl(VAT_AMT,0)-nvl(DISC_AMT,0) net_rt_bill,
       Ad_Date,
       pr_rep
From ias_pos_rt_bill_mst 
Where Nvl(hung,0)= 0
and To_Date(rt_Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Mst.rt_Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Mst.rt_Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Num_of_days_shw_bills,1)
and ( :Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists (Select 1 From User_R Where U_Id=ias_pos_rt_bill_mst.ad_u_id
                 Connect By Prior U_Id = U_Mng Start With U_Id = :Parameter.User_No) )
 Order By Ad_Date desc

Select bill_no    ,
       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       Round(bill_amt+nvl(vat_amt,0)-Nvl(Disc_amt,0),:Parameter.No_Of_Decimal) bill_amt   ,
       Ad_Date    ,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO,
       Brn_No,
       MOBILE_NO
From POS_BILL_MST_ALL_VW
Where Nvl(hung,0)= 0
   AND  NVL(BILL_RTRN,0)=0
  AND  brn_no=:Parameter.brn_no
  And  NVL(MOBILE_NO,'0')=nvl(:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.DMY_MOBILE_NO,NVL(MOBILE_NO,'0'))
  And To_Date(Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.Rt_Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.Rt_Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Change_Return_Period,10)
   And Exists ( Select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv 
	                                 Where S_Brn_Usr_Priv.U_Id    = :Parameter.User_No
	                                   And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No  = POS_BILL_MST_ALL_VW.Brn_No
	                                   And View_Flag =1 
	                                   And Rownum<=1)
 And bill_no not in  ( Select bill_no From POS_RT_BILL_MST_ALL_VW where bill_no  is not null )
  Order By bill_date Desc
Select bill_no    ,
       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       bill_amt,       
       Ad_Date,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO,
       Brn_No,
       MOBILE_NO
 From 
Select bill_no    ,
       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       Round(bill_amt+nvl(vat_amt,0)-Nvl(Disc_amt,0),:Parameter.No_Of_Decimal) bill_amt   ,
       Ad_Date    ,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO,
       Brn_No,
       MOBILE_NO
From POS_BILL_MST_ALL_VW ias_pos_hst_bill_mst 
Where Nvl(hung,0)= 0
   AND  NVL(BILL_RTRN,0)=0
  And To_Date(Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Change_Return_Period,1)
  And Exists ( Select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv 
	                                 Where S_Brn_Usr_Priv.U_Id    = :Parameter.User_No
	                                   And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No  = ias_pos_hst_bill_mst.Brn_No
	                                   And View_Flag =1 
	                                   And Rownum<=1)
Union

       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       Round(bill_amt+nvl(vat_amt,0)-Nvl(Disc_amt,0),:Parameter.No_Of_Decimal) bill_amt   ,
       Ad_Date    ,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO ,
       Brn_no,
       MOBILE_NO
From ias_pos_bill_mst 
Where Nvl(hung,0)= 0
  And NVL(BILL_RTRN,0)=0
  And To_Date(Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Change_Return_Period,1)
  And Exists ( Select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv 
	                                 Where S_Brn_Usr_Priv.U_Id    = :Parameter.User_No
	                                   And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No  = ias_pos_bill_mst.Brn_No
	                                   And View_Flag =1 
	                                   And Rownum<=1)
 Order By Ad_Date  Desc
select m.i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,d.itm_unt unit,m.i_desc 
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
And Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
And Nvl(service_itm,0)=0
and Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(m.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, upper(M.I_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_E_Name),
                3,upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:ias_pos_rt_bill_dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:ias_pos_rt_bill_dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:ias_pos_rt_bill_dtl.I_Code) || '%')
order by Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,i_name,i_e_name),m.i_code
select d.Barcode,m.i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_no,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,d.itm_unt unit,m.i_desc 
 from ias_itm_mst m,Ias_Itm_unt_Barcode d
where  m.I_Code = d.I_Code
And Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1
And RowNum <= 1 )
and m.i_code like  Decode(:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,Null,'%',:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code||'%') 
 order by m.i_code
Select M.Emp_No,Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,Nvl(M.Emp_L_Nm,M.Emp_F_Nm),Nvl(M.Emp_F_Nm,M.Emp_L_Nm)) Emp_Name  From s_Emp M
where Nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0
AND ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or 1 =   (Case When Ys_Gen_Pkg.Get_Fld_Value ('IAS_PARA_GEN', 'EMP_PRV_TYP') = 0
                                         Then 1
                                      Else (Select 1
                                              From S_Emp_Prv
                                             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                                               And Empno_Hrchyno =
                                                      Decode (Emp_Prv_Typ,
                                                              1, M.Emp_No,
                                                              2, M.Hrchy_No
                                                             )
                                               And         Add_Flag=1              
                                               And Rownum <= 1)
                                   End) )
Select Emp_No,Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,Nvl(Emp_L_Nm,Emp_F_Nm),Nvl(Emp_F_Nm,Emp_L_Nm)) Emp_Name
	        From s_Emp
where Nvl(Inactive,0)=0
	        Order By Emp_No
select m.i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,d.itm_unt unit,P_Size,M.i_desc
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
And Nvl(m.service_itm,0)=0
and nvl(d.no_sale,0)=0
and nvl(m.BLOCKED,0)=0
and Nvl(d.INACTIVE,0)=0
and Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=M.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(M.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
and M.I_CODE=:Ias_pos_rt_bill_dtl.i_code
order by Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,i_name,i_e_name),m.i_code

Select   A_Code, Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,
                        1, A_Name,
                        Nvl(A_Name_Eng, A_Name)) A_Name,  
         Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,
                1, Group_Name,
                Group_E_Name) Group_Name
    From Account, Account_Grouping
   Where Account.A_Grouping = Account_Grouping.Group_No(+)
     And Nvl(Account.Ac_Dtl_Typ,0)=Decode(:ias_pos_Rt_bill_mst.AC_DTL_TYP,7,7,0)
     And Exists(Select Account_Type
                  From Account_Types
                 Where Nvl(Affected_By_Trans, 0) = 1 And Account_Type = Account.A_S_M)
     And Exists(
            Select 1
              From Priv_Acc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And A_Code = Account.A_Code
               And Add_Flag = 1
               And Rownum <= 1)
     And A_Code Like Decode(:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.Ac_Code,
                            Null, '%',
                            :Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.Ac_Code || '%')
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                 1, A_Code,
                Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,
                       1, A_Name,
                       A_Name_Eng))
Select EMP_NO,
       Decode (:Parameter.lang_dflt,1, Nvl (EMP_L_NM, EMP_F_NM),
                Nvl (EMP_F_NM, EMP_L_NM)) emp_name
  From S_EMP
 Where  ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (( Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And brn_no= S_EMP.brn_no
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
And  s_emp.EMP_NO Like  Decode(:Ias_pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.ac_code_dtl,Null,'%',:Ias_pos_Rt_Bill_Mst.ac_code_dtl||'%') 
Order By EMP_NO
Select   Customer.C_Code,
         Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,
                1, Nvl(C_A_Name, C_E_Name),
                Nvl(C_E_Name, C_A_Name)) C_Name,
         Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,
                1, Nvl(C_Group_A_Name, C_Group_E_Name),
                Nvl(C_Group_E_Name, C_Group_A_Name)) C_Group_Name,
         C_Phone,
         C_Address
    From Customer,        
         Customer_Group
   Where Customer.C_Group_Code = Customer_Group.C_Group_Code(+)    
     And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or (   (    (:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
                  And Exists(
                         Select 1
                           From Priv_Acc
                          Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                            And A_Code = Customer.C_A_Code
                            And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
                            And Rownum <= 1))
              Or (    (:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
                  And Exists(
                         Select 1
                           From Ias_Priv_Customer
                          Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                            And C_Code = Customer.C_Code
                            And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
                            And Rownum <= 1))))
     And C_Code Like Decode(:Ias_pos_rt_Bill_Mst.Ac_code_dtl,
                            Null, '%',
                            :Ias_pos_rt_Bill_Mst.Ac_code_dtl|| '%')
Order By Lpad( C_Code,'30',0),
         Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,
                1, Nvl(C_A_Name, C_E_Name),
                Nvl(C_E_Name, C_A_Name))
SELECT V_DETAILS.V_CODE,
       DECODE (:PARAMETER.lang_dflt,1, NVL (V_A_NAME, V_E_NAME),
                NVL (V_E_NAME, V_A_NAME)) V_NAME,
       V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE A_CODE
  FROM V_DETAILS
 WHERE V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE=NVL(:IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST.AC_CODE,V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE)
AND ((:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
        OR (((:PARAMETER.APALT = 1)
          AND EXISTS (
                   SELECT 1
                     FROM PRIV_ACC
                    WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                      AND A_CODE = V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE
                      AND NVL(ADD_FLAG,0) = 1 
                      AND ROWNUM <=1 ))
 OR ((:PARAMETER.APALT = 2)
            AND EXISTS (
                   SELECT 1
                     FROM IAS_PRIV_VENDOR
                    WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                      AND V_CODE = V_DETAILS.V_CODE
                      AND NVL(ADD_FLAG,0) = 1
                      AND ROWNUM <=1 ))))
AND  V_CODE LIKE  DECODE(:IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST.AC_CODE_DTL,NULL,'%',:IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST.AC_CODE_DTL||'%') 
ORDER BY LPAD(V_CODE,15,'0') 
Select   D.Ac_Code_Dtl, D.Ac_Dtl_Typ,
         Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,
                 1, Nvl (Ac_Code_Dtl_L_Nm, Ac_Code_Dtl_F_Nm),
                 Nvl (Ac_Code_Dtl_F_Nm, Ac_Code_Dtl_L_Nm)
                ) Ac_Code_Dtl_Nm,
         Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,
                 1, Nvl (Grp_L_Nm, Grp_F_Nm),
                 Nvl (Grp_F_Nm, Grp_L_Nm)
                ) Grp_Nm,
         D.Ac_Code Ac_Code
    From Gls_Accnt_Dtl D, Gls_Ac_Code_Dtl_Grps M
   Where D.Grp_Code = M.Grp_Code
     And D.Ac_Dtl_Typ = M.Ac_Dtl_Typ
     And D.Ac_Dtl_Typ=:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Mst.Ac_Dtl_Typ
     And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or Exists (
                Select 1
                  From Gls_Accnt_Dtl_Priv
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And Ac_Code_Dtl = D.Ac_Code_Dtl
                   And Nvl (Add_Flag, 0) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1)
         )
Order By Lpad (Ac_Code_Dtl, 30, '0')
select a.Barcode,m.i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_no,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,a.itm_unt unit,DECODE (a.expire_date, '01/01/1900', '', a.expire_date) expire_date,
            DECODE (a.batch_no, '0', '', a.batch_no) batch_no 
 from ias_itm_mst m,Ias_Itm_Dtl D,Ias_Itm_Unt_Barcode a
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
And  m.I_Code = a.I_Code
And  d.I_Code = a.I_Code
And  d.Itm_unt = a.Itm_unt
And  m.i_code =:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code
And  a.Itm_unt =nvl(:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Dtl.itm_unt,a.itm_unt)
 order by m.i_code
select m.i_code,TO_Date(d.expire_date,'DD/MM/RRRR') expire_date,
       d.batch_no 
 From ias_itm_mst m,Ias_pos_bill_dtl_tmp d
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
  AND d.BILL_NO=:IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST.BILL_NO 
  AND m.I_CODE =:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code
select  m.i_code,DECODE(1,1,D.I_PRICE_VAT,D.I_PRICE) I_PRICE,SUM(D.i_qty)/COUNT(D.I_CODE) I_QTY,SUM(TMP.I_QTY) RT_QTY
 From ias_itm_mst m,Ias_pos_bill_dtl d,IAS_POS_RT_BILL_DTL_TMP TMP
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
  AND d.BILL_NO=:Ias_Pos_RT_Bill_MST.BILL_NO 
  AND m.I_CODE =:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code
  AND d.itm_unt =:Ias_Pos_rt_Bill_Dtl.Itm_unt
  AND D.Bill_no=TMP.Bill_no(+)
   And D.i_code=TMP.I_CODE(+)
   And D.itm_unt=TMP.itm_unt(+)
   And Round(D.i_price,3)=Round(TMP.i_price(+),3)   
   HAVING SUM(D.I_QTY)/COUNT(D.I_CODE)-SUM(NVL(TMP.I_QTY(+),0))<>0
   GROUP BY m.i_code,DECODE(1,1,D.I_PRICE_VAT,D.I_PRICE) 
select i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,
itm_unt,W_Code,to_date(Expire_Date,'dd/mm/RRRR') Expire_Date,Batch_No,AVL_QTY
From IAS_V_ITM_AVL_QTY
 Where
 W_CODE =DECODE(NVL(:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE,0),0,W_CODE,:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE)
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                3,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Pos_RT_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Pos_Rt_Bill_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
order by i_code,To_Date(Expire_Date,'DD/MM/RRRR'),W_CODE

BATCH_NO

       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Lev_A_Name, Lev_E_Name), Nvl (Lev_E_Name, Lev_A_Name)) L_Name,
       A_Cy,
